entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'circopt.py']
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_check_validation_errors_d0')
case_id = 'declaration_after_assignment'
content = '            input a\n            output y\n            y = a\n            wire t1\n            t1 = a\n            '
error_type = 'DeclarationAfterAssignmentError'

    @pytest.mark.error
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        ("case_id", "content", "error_type"),
        [
            (
                "declaration_after_assignment",
                """\
                input a
                output y
                y = a
                wire t1
                t1 = a
                """,
                "DeclarationAfterAssignmentError",
            ),
            (
                "duplicate_name",
                """\
                input a a
                output y
                y = a
                """,
                "DuplicateNameError",
            ),
            (
                "undefined_name",
                """\
                input a
                output y
                y = z
                """,
                "UndefinedNameError",
            ),
            (
                "input_assignment",
                """\
                input a
                output y
                y = a
                a = 1
                """,
                "InputAssignmentError",
            ),
            (
                "multiple_assignment",
                """\
                input a
                output y
                y = a
                y = NOT(a)
                """,
                "MultipleAssignmentError",
            ),
            (
                "unassigned_signal",
                """\
                input a
                output y
                """,
                "UnassignedSignalError",
            ),
            (
                "duplicate_name_across_lines",
                """\
                input a
                input a
                output y
                y = a
                """,
                "DuplicateNameError",
            ),
            (
                "unassigned_wire",
                """\
                input a
                output y
                wire t1
                y = a
                """,
                "UnassignedSignalError",
            ),
            (
                "undeclared_lhs",
                """\
                input a
                output y
                t1 = a
                y = a
                """,
                "UndefinedNameError",
            ),
        ],
    )
    def test_check_validation_errors(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
        case_id: str,
        content: str,
        error_type: str,
    ) -> None:
        path = write_circ(tmp_path, f"{case_id}.circ", content)

            entrypoint_argv,
            ["check", str(path), "--json"],

        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
        assignments: dict[str, str],
        expected: dict[str, str],
    ) -> None:

        args = ["eval", str(path)]
        for name in ("a", "b", "c"):

            (0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 1),
            # a=0, b=2 -> lt

            # a=0, b=3 -> lt

            # a=3, b=2 -> gt
            (1, 1, 1, 0, 0, 1, 0),
            # a=3, b=3 -> eq
            (1, 1, 1, 1, 1, 0, 0),
        ],
    )
    def test_comparator_2bit_exhaustive(
